BeezUP API

This is the RESTful API of BeezUP which allows you to manage everything related to BeezUP
Contact Info: support@beezup.com
Version: 2.0
BasePath:v2
BeezUP
http://www.beezup.com

Access

  1. APIKey KeyParamName:Ocp-Apim-Subscription-Key KeyInQuery:false KeyInHeader:true

Methods

[ Jump to Models ]

Account

Up 
post /v2/user/customer/account/activate
Activate the user account (activateUserAccount)

Consumes

This API call consumes the following media types via the Content-Type request header:
  • application/json

Request body

emailActivationId string (required)
Body Parameter — The email activation id received by email.

Produces

This API call produces the following media types according to the Accept request header; the media type will be conveyed by the Content-Type response header.
  • application/json

Responses

204

User account activated

403

Invalid email activation id

0

Occurs when something goes wrong BeezUP.Common.ErrorResponseMessage
Up 
post /v2/user/customer/account/changePassword
Change user password (changePassword)

Consumes

This API call consumes the following media types via the Content-Type request header:
  • application/json

Request body

request ChangePasswordRequest (required)
Body Parameter —

Produces

This API call produces the following media types according to the Accept request header; the media type will be conveyed by the Content-Type response header.
  • application/json

Responses

204

Password updated

400

Old password is invalid or the new password does not respect the password's constraints

0

Occurs when something goes wrong BeezUP.Common.ErrorResponseMessage

post /v2/user/customer/account/resendEmailActivation
Resend email activation (resendEmailActivation)

Consumes

This API call consumes the following media types via the Content-Type request header:
  • application/json

Produces

This API call produces the following media types according to the Accept request header; the media type will be conveyed by the Content-Type response header.
  • application/json

Responses

204

Email activation resent

400

Email activation not sent because of email problem. Ensure that your email is the correct one.

403

Email activation sent recently, must retry later. (One per hour)

502

Email activate send failed because of our email service. Ensure that your email is the correct one otherwise please contact our support if the problem persists.

0

Occurs when something goes wrong BeezUP.Common.ErrorResponseMessage
Up

Alerts

get /v2/user/customer/stores/{storeId}/alerts
Get store's alerts (getStoreAlerts)

Path parameters

storeId (required)
Path Parameter — Your store identifier format: guid

Consumes

This API call consumes the following media types via the Content-Type request header:
  • application/json

Return type

storeAlerts

Example data

Content-Type: application/json
{
  "alerts" : [ {
    "alertId" : 8,
    "alertName" : "NoImportSinceXDays",
    "isActive" : true,
    "properties" : [ {
      "propertyId" : 2,
      "propertyValidationExpression" : "\\b0*([1-9]|[12][0-9]|30)\\b",
      "propertyValue" : 2
    } ]
  } ]
}

Produces

This API call produces the following media types according to the Accept request header; the media type will be conveyed by the Content-Type response header.
  • application/json

Responses

200

User account alerts information storeAlerts

404

Store not found or not authorized

0

Occurs when something goes wrong BeezUP.Common.ErrorResponseMessage

costType - Up

CPC means cost per click. CPA means cost per action. You can have CPC/CPA with a global cost value. You can have CPC/CPA by category the cost value MUST be null You can have global fixed price.

trackedExternalOrderProduct - Up

productSku
String The product sku received related to the external order.
productTitle (optional)
String We tried to get the catalog product title based on the product SKU. This property can be null, if we cannot found the product. This is possible if the product is not referenced in the imported catalog.
productImageUrl (optional)
String We tried to get the catalog product image Url based on the product SKU. This property can be null, if we cannot found the product. This is possible if the product is not referenced in the imported catalog. format: uri
productActive (optional)
Boolean We tried to get the catalog product if it's still active based on the product SKU. This property can be null, if we cannot found the product. This is possible if the product is not referenced in the imported catalog.
productId (optional)
String We tried to get the catalog product identifier based on the product SKU. This property can be null, if we cannot found the product. This is possible if the product is not referenced in the imported catalog. format: guid
unitPrice (optional)
String The product's unit price related to this external order. This property is voluntarily a string because the value could be an invalid one.
quantity (optional)
String Indicate the product's quantity ordered. This property is voluntarily a string because the value could be an invalid one
margin (optional)
String Indicate the product's margin related to this order. This property is voluntarily a string because the value could be an invalid one
